# Joint probabilities with integer values

This is me getting obsessed with the shape created by drawing joint probabilities such that the areas and lengths are proportional to the probabilities they represent.

Legend:
- a = first random variable
- b = second random variable
- b|a = probability of b given a
- b|na = probability of b given not a
- a|b = probability of a given b
- a|nb = probability of a given not b

How to read the ascii art:
```
       b|a   ~b|a                   b     ~b
                                  
          |                            |     
          |                 a|b    a&b |     
   a   a&b|  a&~b                      |     
          |                       -----+ a&~b    a|~b
          |                            |     
       ---+---+---                     |     
              |                        |     
              |            ~a|b   ~a&b +-----
  ~a    ~a&b  |~a&~b                   |     
              |                        | ~a&~b  ~a|~b
              |                        |     

        b|~a   ~b|~a    
```

I looked for all such squares for 2x2 to 100x100 grids such that:
- All probability values were nice (integers)
- For symmetry normalization: p(a&~b) >= p(a&b), p(~a&b), p(~a&~b)
- For symmetry normalization: p(a&b) >= p(~a&~b)

```
```
## 4x4 -- 1 squares found --
```

tu=4	a=2,b|a=1,b|na=3	b=2.0,a|b=1.0,a|nb=3.0
 |         |  
 |       --+  
-+-+-      |  
   |       +--
   |       |  


```
